# Custom domain - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Core configuration

Custom domain

To set up your documentation on a custom domain, you’ll need to set your desired custom domain in your Mintlify settings and configure your DNS settings on your domain provider.

Looking to set up a custom subdirectory like `mintlify.com/docs`? See the [custom subdirectory](https://mintlify.com/docs/advanced/subpath/cloudflare)
 docs.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-domain#dashboard-settings)

Dashboard settings
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Navigate to your [dashboard](https://dashboard.mintlify.com/)
    
2.  Select **Settings**
3.  Select **Domain Setup**
4.  Enter your desired custom domain. For example, `docs.mintlify.com`

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-domain#configuring-your-dns)

Configuring your DNS
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Proceed to your domain’s DNS settings on your domain provider’s website.
2.  Create a new DNS entry, inputting the following values:

Copy

Ask AI

    CNAME | docs | cname.vercel-dns.com.
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-domain#provider-specific-settings)

Provider-specific settings
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Vercel verification

If Vercel is your domain provider, you must add a verification `TXT` record. This information will show on your dashboard after submitting your custom domain, as well as be emailed to you.

Cloudflare security settings

If Cloudflare is your DNS provider, you must enable the “full strict” security option for the https setting.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Previous](https://mintlify.com/docs/themes)
[AI ingestionPrepare your documentation for LLMs and AI tools\
\
Next](https://mintlify.com/docs/ai-ingestion)

*   [Dashboard settings](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-domain#dashboard-settings)
    
*   [Configuring your DNS](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-domain#configuring-your-dns)

# Images and embeds - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Components

Images and embeds

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#images)

Images
------------------------------------------------------------

Add images to provide visual context, examples, or decoration to your documentation.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#basic-image-syntax)

Basic image syntax

Use [Markdown syntax](https://www.markdownguide.org/basic-syntax/#images)
 to add images to your documentation:

Copy

Ask AI

    ![Alt text describing the image](/path/to/image.png)
    

Always include descriptive alt text to improve accessibility and SEO. The alt text should clearly describe what the image shows.

Image files must be less than 20MB. For larger files, host them on a CDN service like [Amazon S3](https://aws.amazon.com/s3)
 or [Cloudinary](https://cloudinary.com/)
.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#html-image-embeds)

HTML image embeds

For more control over image display, use HTML `<img>` tags:

Copy

Ask AI

    <img 
      src="/images/dashboard.png" 
      alt="Main dashboard interface"
      height="300"
      className="rounded-lg"
    />
    

#### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#disable-zoom-functionality)

Disable zoom functionality

To disable the default zoom on click for images, add the `noZoom` property:

Copy

Ask AI

    <img 
      src="/images/screenshot.png" 
      alt="Descriptive alt text"
      noZoom 
      height="200"
    />
    

#### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#link-images)

Link images

To make an image a clickable link, wrap the image in an anchor tag and add the `noZoom` property:

Copy

Ask AI

    <a href="https://mintlify.com" target="_blank">
      <img 
        src="/images/logo.png" 
        alt="Mintlify logo"
        noZoom 
        height="100"
      />
    </a>
    

Images within anchor tags automatically display a pointer cursor to indicate they are clickable.

#### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#light-and-dark-mode-images)

Light and dark mode images

To display different images for light and dark themes, use Tailwind CSS classes:

Copy

Ask AI

    <!-- Light mode image -->
    <img 
      className="block dark:hidden" 
      src="/images/light-mode.png" 
      alt="Light mode interface"
    />
    
    <!-- Dark mode image -->
    <img 
      className="hidden dark:block" 
      src="/images/dark-mode.png" 
      alt="Dark mode interface"
    />
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#videos)

Videos
------------------------------------------------------------

Mintlify supports [HTML tags in Markdown](https://www.markdownguide.org/basic-syntax/#html)
, giving you flexibility to create rich content.

Always include fallback text content within video elements for browsers that don’t support video playback.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#youtube-embeds)

YouTube embeds

Embed YouTube videos using iframe elements:

Copy

Ask AI

    <iframe
      className="w-full aspect-video rounded-xl"
      src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/4KzFe50RQkQ"
      title="YouTube video player"
      frameBorder="0"
      allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture"
      allowFullScreen
    ></iframe>
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#self-hosted-videos)

Self-hosted videos

Use the HTML `<video>` element for self-hosted video content:

Copy

Ask AI

    <video
      controls
      className="w-full aspect-video rounded-xl"
      src="link-to-your-video.com"
    ></video>
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#autoplay-videos)

Autoplay videos

To autoplay a video, use:

Copy

Ask AI

    <video
      autoPlay
      muted
      loop
      playsInline
      className="w-full aspect-video rounded-xl"
      src="/videos/demo.mp4"
    ></video>
    

When using JSX syntax, write double-word attributes in camelCase: `autoPlay`, `playsInline`, `allowFullScreen`.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#iframes)

iframes
--------------------------------------------------------------

Embed external content using iframe elements:

Copy

Ask AI

    <iframe 
      src="https://example.com/embed" 
      title="Embedded content"
      className="w-full h-96 rounded-xl"
    ></iframe>
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds#related-resources)

Related resources
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Frame component reference\
-------------------------\
\
Learn how to use the Frame component for presenting images.](https://mintlify.com/docs/components/frames)

# Redirects and broken links - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Guides

Redirects and broken links

When you change the path of a file in your docs folder, it will also change the path of the URL to that page. This may happen when restructuring your docs or changing the sidebar title.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/broken-links#broken-links)

Broken Links
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Catch broken links with our CLI. Simply [install the CLI](https://mintlify.com/docs/installation)
 and run the command:

Copy

Ask AI

    mint broken-links
    

The CLI will identify any relative links in your docs that don’t exist.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/broken-links#redirects)

Redirects
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set up 301 redirects by adding the `redirects` field into your `docs.json` file.

Copy

Ask AI

    "redirects": [\
      {\
        "source": "/source/path",\
        "destination": "/destination/path"\
      }\
    ]
    

This will permanently redirect `/source/path` to `/destination/path` so that you don’t lose any previous SEO for the original page.

To match a wildcard path, use `*` after a parameter. In this example, `/beta/:slug*` will match `/beta/introduction` and redirects it to `/v2/introduction`.

Copy

Ask AI

    "redirects": [\
      {\
        "source": "/beta/:slug*",\
        "destination": "/v2/:slug*"\
      }\
    ]
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Previous](https://mintlify.com/docs/guides/hidden-pages)
[Monorepo setupDeploy your docs from a repo that contains multiple projects\
\
Next](https://mintlify.com/docs/guides/monorepo)

On this page

*   [Broken Links](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/broken-links#broken-links)
    
*   [Redirects](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/broken-links#redirects)

# Custom scripts - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

⌘KAsk AI

Navigation

Guides

Custom scripts

Use CSS to style HTML elements or add custom CSS and JavaScript to fully customize the look and feel of your documentation.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-scripts#styling-with-tailwind-css)

Styling with Tailwind CSS
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use Tailwind CSS v3 to style HTML elements. You can control layout, spacing, colors, and other visual properties. Some common classes are:

*   `w-full` - Full width
*   `aspect-video` - 16:9 aspect ratio
*   `rounded-xl` - Large rounded corners
*   `block`, `hidden` - Display control
*   `dark:hidden`, `dark:block` - Dark mode visibility

Tailwind CSS arbitrary values are not supported. For custom values, use the `style` prop instead.

Copy

Ask AI

    <img style={{ width: '350px', margin: '12px auto' }} src="/path/image.jpg" />
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-scripts#custom-css)

Custom CSS
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add CSS files to your repository and their defined class names will be applied and available in all of your `MDX` files.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-scripts#adding-style-css)

Adding `style.css`

For example, you can add the following `style.css` file to customize the styling of the navbar and footer.

Copy

Ask AI

    #navbar {
      background: "#fffff2";
      padding: 1rem;
    }
    
    footer {
      margin-top: 2rem;
    }
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-scripts#using-identifiers-and-selectors)

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-scripts#custom-javascript)

Custom JavaScript
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Custom JS allows you to add custom executable code globally. It is the equivalent of adding a `<script>` tag with JS code into every page.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/custom-scripts#adding-custom-javascript)

Adding custom JavaScript

Any `.js` file inside the content directory of your docs will be included in every documentation page. For example, you can add the following `ga.js` file to enable [Google Analytics](https://marketingplatform.google.com/about/analytics)
 across the entire documentation.

Copy

Ask AI

    window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
    function gtag() {
      dataLayer.push(arguments);
    }
    gtag('js', new Date());
    
    gtag('config', 'TAG_ID');
    

Please use with caution to not introduce security vulnerabilities.

# Model Context Protocol - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Guides

Model Context Protocol

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#overview)

Overview
-------------------------------------------------------

The Model Context Protocol (MCP) is an open protocol that connects your functions to LLMs and AI applications. With Mintlify’s integration, you can automatically generate an MCP server from your existing documentation or OpenAPI specifications, enabling seamless AI-powered interactions with your product.

MCP servers can only be generated for public documentation. Documentation behind end-user authentication cannot be accessed for server generation.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#generating-your-mcp-server)

Generating your MCP server
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Public documentation hosted on Mintlify can be extracted as an MCP server using the following command:

Copy

Ask AI

    npx mint-mcp add <your-subdomain-or-domain>
    

Examples:

Copy

Ask AI

    # Using subdomain
    npx mint-mcp add mintlify
    
    # Using domain
    npx mint-mcp add mintlify.com
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#authentication)

Authentication

When you run the command, you’ll need to provide two API keys, `External Admin Key` and `Assistant API Key`.

These can be found in your [dashboard](https://dashboard.mintlify.com/settings/organization/api-keys)
 under **Settings > API Keys**.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#select-mcp-clients)

Select MCP clients

After authentication, you’ll choose which MCP clients to enable for your server:

Once configured, your MCP server is ready to use with the command provided in the terminal.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#configuring-your-mcp-server)

Configuring your MCP server
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Now let’s take a look at how to configure your MCP server.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#default-functionality)

Default functionality

All MCP servers include the `search` tool by default, allowing users to query information across your entire documentation.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#adding-api-functions)

Adding API functions

If you have an OpenAPI specification, you can expose specific endpoints as MCP tools by using the `x-mcp` extension at either the file or endpoint level.

#### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#file-level-configuration)

File-level configuration

Enable MCP for all endpoints in a specification file:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "openapi": "3.1.0",
      "x-mcp": {
        "enabled": true
      },
      // Other OpenAPI content
    }
    

#### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#endpoint-level-configuration)

Endpoint-level configuration

Enable MCP for specific endpoints only:

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "paths": {
        "/api/v1/users": {
          "x-mcp": {
            "enabled": true
          },
          // Endpoint configuration
        }
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#authentication-handling)

Authentication handling

If your OpenAPI spec defines authentication using `securitySchemes`, these authentication methods will be automatically applied to your MCP server.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#monitoring-your-mcp-server)

Monitoring your MCP server

After publishing your changes, you can view all available MCP tools in the **Available Tools** section on the MCP server page in your dashboard.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#distribution)

Distribution
---------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/mcp#user-installation)

User installation

Your users can install and use your MCP server with:

Copy

Ask AI

    npx mint-mcp add <your-subdomain-or-domain>
    

This provides them with a ready-to-use MCP server that connects your documented functions to AI applications.

YesNo

\

# Reusable snippets - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Components

Reusable snippets

One of the core principles of software development is DRY (Don’t Repeat Yourself), which applies to documentation as well. If you find yourself repeating the same content in multiple places, you should create a custom snippet to keep your content in sync.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#creating-a-custom-snippet)

Creating a custom snippet
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Pre-condition**: You must create your snippet file in the `snippets` directory in order for the import to work.

Any page in the `snippets` directory will be treated as a snippet and will not be rendered into a standalone page. If you want to create a standalone page from the snippet, import the snippet into another file and call it as a component.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#default-export)

Default export

1.  Add content to your snippet file that you want to re-use. Optionally, you can add variables that can be filled in via props when you import the snippet. In this example, our variable is word.

snippets/my-snippet.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    Hello world! This is my content I want to reuse across pages. 
    

2.  Import the snippet into your destination file.

destination-file.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: My title
    description: My Description
    ---
    
    import MySnippet from '/snippets/path/to/my-snippet.mdx';
    
    ## Header
    
    Lorem impsum dolor sit amet.
    
    <MySnippet/>
    
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#exporting-with-variables)

Exporting with variables

1.  Optionally, you can add variables that can be filled in via props when you import the snippet. In this example, our variable is word.

snippets/my-snippet.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    My keyword of the day is {word}.
    

2.  Import the snippet into your destination file with the variable. The property will fill in based on your specification.

destination-file.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: My title
    description: My Description
    ---
    
    import MySnippet from '/snippets/path/to/my-snippet.mdx';
    
    ## Header
    
    Lorem impsum dolor sit amet.
    
    <MySnippet word="bananas" />
    
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#reusable-variables)

Reusable variables

1.  Export a variable from your snippet file:

snippets/path/to/custom-variables.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    export const myName = 'my name';
    
    export const myObject = { fruit: 'strawberries' };
    

2.  Import the snippet from your destination file and use the variable:

destination-file.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: My title
    description: My Description
    ---
    
    import { myName, myObject } from '/snippets/path/to/custom-variables.mdx';
    
    Hello, my name is {myName} and I like {myObject.fruit}.
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#jsx-snippets)

JSX snippets

1.  Export a JSX component from your snippet file. (See [React components](https://mintlify.com/docs/react-components)
     for more information):

snippets/my-jsx-snippet.jsx

Copy

Ask AI

    export const MyJSXSnippet = () => {
      return (
        <div>
          <h1>Hello, world!</h1>
        </div>
      )
    }
    

Important: When creating JSX snippets, use arrow function syntax (`=>`) rather than function declarations. The `function` keyword is not supported in this context.

2.  Import the snippet from your destination file and use the component:

destination-file.mdx

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: My title
    description: My Description
    ---
    
    import { MyJSXSnippet } from '/snippets/my-jsx-snippet.jsx';
    
    <MyJSXSnippet />
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Previous](https://mintlify.com/docs/code)
[AccordionsA dropdown component to toggle content visibility\
\
Next](https://mintlify.com/docs/components/accordions)

On this page

*   [Creating a custom snippet](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#creating-a-custom-snippet)
    
*   [Default export](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#default-export)
    
*   [Exporting with variables](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#exporting-with-variables)
    
*   [Reusable variables](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#reusable-variables)
    
*   [JSX snippets](https://mintlify.com/docs/reusable-snippets#jsx-snippets)

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.

# Headers and text - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Components

Headers and text

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#headers)

Headers
------------------------------------------------------

Headers organize your content and create navigation anchors. They appear in the table of contents and help users scan your documentation.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#creating-headers)

Creating headers

Use `#` symbols to create headers of different levels:

Copy

Ask AI

    ## Main section header
    ### Subsection header
    #### Sub-subsection header
    

Use descriptive, keyword-rich headers that clearly indicate the content that follows. This improves both user navigation and search engine optimization.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#text-formatting)

Text formatting
----------------------------------------------------------------------

We support most Markdown formatting for emphasizing and styling text.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#basic-formatting)

Basic formatting

Apply these formatting styles to your text:

| Style | Syntax | Example | Result |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Bold** | `**text**` | `**important note**` | **important note** |
| _Italic_ | `_text_` | `_emphasis_` | _emphasis_ |
| ~Strikethrough~ | `~text~` | `~deprecated feature~` | ~deprecated feature~ |

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#combining-formats)

Combining formats

You can combine formatting styles:

Copy

Ask AI

    **_bold and italic_**
    **~~bold and strikethrough~~**
    *~~italic and strikethrough~~**
    

_**bold and italic**_  
**~bold and strikethrough~**  
_~italic and strikethrough~_

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#superscript-and-subscript)

Superscript and subscript

For mathematical expressions or footnotes, use HTML tags:

| Type | Syntax | Example | Result |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Superscript | `<sup>text</sup>` | `example<sup>2</sup>` | example2 |
| Subscript | `<sub>text</sub>` | `example<sub>n</sub>` | examplen |

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#links)

Links
--------------------------------------------------

Links help users navigate between pages and access external resources. Use descriptive link text to improve accessibility and user experience.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#internal-links)

Internal links

Link to other pages in your documentation using root-relative paths:

Copy

Ask AI

    [Quickstart](/quickstart)
    [Steps](/components/steps)
    

[Quickstart](https://mintlify.com/docs/quickstart)
  
[Steps](https://mintlify.com/docs/components/steps)

Avoid relative links like `[page](../page)` as they load slower and cannot be optimized as effectively as root-relative links.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#external-links)

External links

For external resources, include the full URL:

Copy

Ask AI

    [Markdown Guide](https://www.markdownguide.org/)
    

[Markdown Guide](https://www.markdownguide.org/)

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#broken-links)

Broken links

You can check for broken links in your documentation using the [CLI](https://mintlify.com/docs/installation)
:

Copy

Ask AI

    mint broken-links
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#blockquotes)

Blockquotes
--------------------------------------------------------------

Blockquotes highlight important information, quotes, or examples within your content.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#single-line-blockquotes)

Single line blockquotes

Add `>` before text to create a blockquote:

Copy

Ask AI

    > This is a quote that stands out from the main content.
    

> This is a quote that stands out from the main content.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#multi-line-blockquotes)

Multi-line blockquotes

For longer quotes or multiple paragraphs:

Copy

Ask AI

    > This is the first paragraph of a multi-line blockquote.
    >
    > This is the second paragraph, separated by an empty line with `>`.
    

> This is the first paragraph of a multi-line blockquote.
> 
> This is the second paragraph, separated by an empty line with `>`.

Use blockquotes sparingly to maintain their visual impact and meaning. Consider using [callouts](https://mintlify.com/docs/components/callouts)
 for notes, warnings, and other information.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#mathematical-expressions)

Mathematical expressions
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We support LaTeX for rendering mathematical expressions and equations.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#inline-math)

Inline math

Use single dollar signs, `$`, for inline mathematical expressions:

Copy

Ask AI

    The Pythagorean theorem states that $(a^2 + b^2 = c^2)$ in a right triangle.
    

The Pythagorean theorem states that (a2+b2\=c2)(a^2 + b^2 = c^2)(a2+b2\=c2) in a right triangle.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#block-equations)

Block equations

Use double dollar signs, `$$`, for standalone equations:

Copy

Ask AI

    $$
    E = mc^2
    $$
    

E\=mc2E = mc^2E\=mc2

LaTeX support requires proper mathematical syntax. Refer to the [LaTeX documentation](https://www.latex-project.org/help/documentation/)
 for comprehensive syntax guidelines.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#line-breaks-and-spacing)

Line breaks and spacing
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Control spacing and line breaks to improve content readability.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#paragraph-breaks)

Paragraph breaks

Separate paragraphs with blank lines:

Copy

Ask AI

    This is the first paragraph.
    
    This is the second paragraph, separated by a blank line.
    

This is the first paragraph.

This is the second paragraph, separated by a blank line.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#manual-line-breaks)

Manual line breaks

Use HTML `<br />` tags for forced line breaks within paragraphs:

Copy

Ask AI

    This line ends here.<br />
    This line starts on a new line.
    

This line ends here.  
This line starts on a new line.

In most cases, paragraph breaks with blank lines provide better readability than manual line breaks.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#best-practices)

Best practices
--------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#content-organization)

Content organization

*   Use headers to create clear content hierarchy
*   Follow proper header hierarchy (don’t skip from H2 to H4)
*   Write descriptive, keyword-rich header text

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#text-formatting-2)

Text formatting

*   Use bold for emphasis, not for entire paragraphs
*   Reserve italics for terms, titles, or subtle emphasis
*   Avoid over-formatting that distracts from content

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#links-2)

Links

*   Write descriptive link text instead of “click here” or “read more”
*   Use root-relative paths for internal links
*   Test links regularly to prevent broken references

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Previous](https://mintlify.com/docs/ai-ingestion)
[Images and embedsAdd images, videos, and iframes\
\
Next](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds)

On this page

*   [Headers](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#headers)

*   [Text formatting](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#text-formatting)

*   [Links](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#links)
    
*   [Internal links](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#internal-links)
    
*   [External links](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#external-links)
    
*   [Broken links](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#broken-links)
    
*   [Blockquotes](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#blockquotes)
    
*   [Single line blockquotes](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#single-line-blockquotes)
    
*   [Multi-line blockquotes](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#multi-line-blockquotes)
    
*   [Mathematical expressions](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#mathematical-expressions)

*   [Best practices](https://mintlify.com/docs/text#best-practices)

# Code - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Components

Code

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#adding-code-samples)

Adding code samples
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add inline code snippets or code blocks. Code blocks support meta options for syntax highlighting, titles, line highlighting, icons, and more.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#inline-code)

Inline code

To denote a `word` or `phrase` as code, enclose it in backticks (\`).

Copy

Ask AI

    To denote a `word` or `phrase` as code, enclose it in backticks (`).
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#code-blocks)

Code blocks

Use [fenced code blocks](https://www.markdownguide.org/extended-syntax/#fenced-code-blocks)
 by enclosing code in three backticks. Code blocks are copyable, and if you have the assistant enabled, users can ask AI to explain the code.

Specify the programming language for syntax highlighting and to enable meta options. Add any meta options, like a title or icon, after the language.

HelloWorld.java

Copy

Ask AI

    class HelloWorld {
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println("Hello, World!");
        }
    }
    

Copy

Ask AI

    ```java HelloWorld.java lines icon="java"
    class HelloWorld {
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println("Hello, World!");
        }
    }
    ```
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#code-block-options)

Code block options
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can add meta options to your code blocks to customize their appearance.

You must specify a programming language for a code block before adding any other meta options.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#option-syntax)

Option syntax

*   **String and boolean options**: Wrap with `""`, `''`, or no quotes.
*   **Expression options**: Wrap with `{}`, `""`, or `''`.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#syntax-highlighting)

Syntax highlighting

Enable syntax highlighting by specifying the programming language after the opening backticks of a code block.

We use [Shiki](https://shiki.style/)
 for syntax highlighting and support all available languages. See the full list of [languages](https://shiki.style/languages)
 in Shiki’s documentation.

Copy

Ask AI

    class HelloWorld {
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println("Hello, World!");
        }
    }
    

Copy

Ask AI

    ```java
    class HelloWorld {
        public static void main(String[] args) {
            System.out.println("Hello, World!");
        }
    }
    ```
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#title)

Title

Add a title to label your code example. Use `title="Your title"` or a string on a single line.

Code Block Example

Copy

Ask AI

    const hello = "world";
    

Copy

Ask AI

    ```javascript Code Block Example
    const hello = "world";
    ```
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#icon)

Icon

Add an icon to your code block. You can use [FontAwesome](https://fontawesome.com/icons)
 icons, [Lucide](https://lucide.dev/icons/)
 icons, or absolute URLs.

Copy

Ask AI

    const hello = "world";
    

Copy

Ask AI

    ```javascript icon="square-js"
    const hello = "world";
    ```
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#line-highlighting)

Line Highlighting

Highlight specific lines in your code blocks using `highlight` with the line numbers or ranges you want to highlight.

Line Highlighting Example

Copy

Ask AI

    const greeting = "Hello, World!";
    function sayHello() {
      console.log(greeting);
    }
    sayHello();
    

Copy

Ask AI

    ```javascript Line Highlighting Example highlight={1-2,5}
    const greeting = "Hello, World!";
    function sayHello() {
      console.log(greeting);
    }
    sayHello();
    ```

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#expandable)

Expandable

Allow users to expand and collapse long code blocks using `expandable`.

Expandable Example

Copy

Ask AI

    from datetime import datetime, timedelta
    from typing import Dict, List, Optional
    from dataclasses import dataclass
    
    @dataclass
    class Book:
        title: str
        author: str
        isbn: str
        checked_out: bool = False
        due_date: Optional[datetime] = None
    
    class Library:
        def __init__(self):
            self.books: Dict[str, Book] = {}
            self.checkouts: Dict[str, List[str]] = {}  # patron -> list of ISBNs
    
        def add_book(self, book: Book) -> None:
            if book.isbn in self.books:
                raise ValueError(f"Book with ISBN {book.isbn} already exists")
            self.books[book.isbn] = book
    
        def checkout_book(self, isbn: str, patron: str, days: int = 14) -> None:
            if patron not in self.checkouts:
                self.checkouts[patron] = []
    
            book = self.books.get(isbn)
            if not book:
                raise ValueError("Book not found")
    
            if book.checked_out:
                raise ValueError("Book is already checked out")
    
            if len(self.checkouts[patron]) >= 3:
                raise ValueError("Patron has reached checkout limit")
    
            book.checked_out = True
            book.due_date = datetime.now() + timedelta(days=days)
            self.checkouts[patron].append(isbn)
    
        def return_book(self, isbn: str) -> float:
            book = self.books.get(isbn)
            if not book or not book.checked_out:
                raise ValueError("Book not found or not checked out")
    
            late_fee = 0.0
            if datetime.now() > book.due_date:
                days_late = (datetime.now() - book.due_date).days
                late_fee = days_late * 0.50
    
            book.checked_out = False
            book.due_date = None
    
            # Remove from patron's checkouts
            for patron, books in self.checkouts.items():
                if isbn in books:
                    books.remove(isbn)
                    break
    
            return late_fee
    
        def search(self, query: str) -> List[Book]:
            query = query.lower()
            return [\
                book for book in self.books.values()\
                if query in book.title.lower() or query in book.author.lower()\
            ]
    
    def main():
        library = Library()
    
        # Add some books
        books = [\
            Book("The Hobbit", "J.R.R. Tolkien", "978-0-261-10295-4"),\
            Book("1984", "George Orwell", "978-0-452-28423-4"),\
        ]
    
        for book in books:
            library.add_book(book)
    
        # Checkout and return example
        library.checkout_book("978-0-261-10295-4", "patron123")
        late_fee = library.return_book("978-0-261-10295-4")
        print(f"Late fee: ${late_fee:.2f}")
    
    if __name__ == "__main__":
        main()
    

See all 87 lines

Copy

Ask AI

    ```python Expandable Example expandable
    from datetime import datetime, timedelta
    from typing import Dict, List, Optional
    from dataclasses import dataclass
    
    # ...
    
    if __name__ == "__main__":
        main()
    ```
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#wrap)

Wrap

Enable text wrapping for long lines using `wrap`. This prevents horizontal scrolling and makes long lines easier to read.

Wrap Example

Copy

Ask AI

    const greeting = "Hello, World! I am a long line of text that will wrap to the next line.";
    function sayHello() {
      console.log(greeting);
    }
    sayHello();
    

Copy

Ask AI

    ```javascript Wrap Example wrap
    const greeting = "Hello, World! I am a long line of text that will wrap to the next line.";
    function sayHello() {
      console.log(greeting);
    }
    sayHello();
    ```
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/code#diff)

Diff

Add single line comments with `[!code ++]` and `[!code --]` to mark added and removed lines. You can also mark multiple lines with a single comment, such as `[!code ++:3]` or `[!code --:5]`.

Diff Example

Copy

Ask AI

    const greeting = "Hello, World!"; 
    function sayHello() {
      console.log("Hello, World!"); 
      console.log(greeting); 
    }
    sayHello();
    

Copy

Ask AI

    ```js Diff Example icon="code" lines
    const greeting = "Hello, World!"; // [\!code ++]
    function sayHello() {
      console.log("Hello, World!"); // [\!code --]
      console.log(greeting); // [\!code ++]
    }
    sayHello();
    ```

# Navigation - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Core configuration

Navigation

The [navigation](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings#param-navigation)
 property in [docs.json](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings)
 defines how users will browse through your documentation. Think of it as the blueprint for your documentation’s menu structure.

With proper navigation configuration, you can organize your content into a logical hierarchy that makes it easy for users to find exactly what they’re looking for.

Do not use `api` as a title for any navigation element. The `/api` path is reserved in production and will cause pages to return 404 errors if their URLs contain `/api`.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/navigation#pages)

Pages
--------------------------------------------------------

Pages are the most fundamental navigation component.

Pages is an array where each entry must be a reference to the path of a [page file](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages)
.

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "navigation": {
        "pages": [\
          "overview",\
          "quickstart",\
          "advanced/components",\
          "advanced/integrations"\
        ]
      }
    }
    

* * *

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/navigation#groups)

Groups
----------------------------------------------------------

Use groups to organize your navigation into sections. Groups can be nested within each other, labeled with tags, and styled with icons.

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "navigation": {
        "groups": [\
          {\
            "group": "Getting Started",\
    		"icon": "play",\
            "pages": [\
              "quickstart",\
              {\
                "group": "Editing",\
    			"icon": "pencil",\
                "pages": [\
    				"installation",\
    				"editor",\
    				{\
    					"group": "Nested group",\
    					"icon": "code",\
    					"pages": [\
    						"navigation",\
    						"code"\
    					]\
    				}\
    			]\
              }\
            ]\
          },\
          {\
            "group": "Writing Content",\
     		"icon": "notebook-text",\
            "tag": "NEW",\
            "pages": ["writing-content/page", "writing-content/text"]\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/navigation#tabs)

Tabs
------------------------------------------------------

Tabs help distinguish between different topics or sections of your documentation.

Copy

Ask AI

    "navigation": {
      "tabs": [\
        {\
          "tab": "API References",\
          "pages": [\
            "api-reference/get",\
            "api-reference/post",\
            "api-reference/delete"\
          ]\
        },\
        {\
          "tab": "SDKs",\
          "pages": [\
            "sdk/fetch",\
            "sdk/create",\
            "sdk/delete",\
          ]\
        },\
        {\
          "tab": "Blog",\
          "href": "https://external-link.com/blog"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

* * *

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/navigation#anchors)

Anchors
------------------------------------------------------------

Anchors are another way to section your content. They show up on top of your side navigation.

The configuration is very similar to tabs.

While not required, we highly recommend that you set an `icon` field as well.

Copy

Ask AI

    "navigation": {
      "anchors": [\
        {\
          "anchor": "Documentation",\
          "icon": "book-open",\
          "pages": [\
            "quickstart",\
            "development",\
            "navigation"\
          ]\
        },\
        {\
          "anchor": "API References",\
          "icon": "square-terminal",\
          "pages": [\
            "api-reference/get",\
            "api-reference/post",\
            "api-reference/delete"\
          ]\
        },\
        {\
          "anchor": "Blog",\
          "href": "https://external-link.com/blog"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

* * *

Anchors that strictly contain external links can be achieved using the `global` keyword:

Copy

Ask AI

    "navigation": {
      "global":  {
        "anchors": [\
          {\
             "anchor": "Community",\
             "icon": "house",\
             "href": "https://slack.com"\
          },\
          {\
             "anchor": "Blog",\
             "icon": "pencil",\
             "href": "https://mintlify.com/blog"\
          }\
        ]
      },
      "tabs": /*...*/
    }
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/navigation#dropdowns)

Dropdowns
----------------------------------------------------------------

Dropdowns show up in the same place as anchors, but are consolidated into a single dropdown.

While not required, we also recommend that you set an icon for each dropdown item.

Copy

Ask AI

    "navigation": {
      "dropdowns": [\
        {\
          "dropdown": "Documentation",\
          "icon": "book-open",\
          "pages": [\
            "quickstart",\
            "development",\
            "navigation"\
          ]\
        }\
        {\
          "dropdown": "API References",\
          "icon": "square-terminal",\
          "pages": [\
            "api-reference/get",\
            "api-reference/post",\
            "api-reference/delete"\
          ]\
        }\
        {\
          "dropdown": "Blog",\
          "href": "https://external-link.com/blog"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

* * *

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/navigation#versions)

Versions
--------------------------------------------------------------

Versions can be leveraged to partition your navigation into different versions.

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "navigation": {
        "versions": [\
          {\
            "version": "1.0.0",\
            "groups": [\
              {\
                "group": "Getting Started",\
                "pages": ["v1/overview", "v1/quickstart", "v1/development"]\
              }\
            ]\
          },\
          {\
            "version": "2.0.0",\
            "groups": [\
              {\
                "group": "Getting Started",\
                "pages": ["v2/overview", "v2/quickstart", "v2/development"]\
              }\
            ]\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

* * *

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/navigation#languages)

Languages
----------------------------------------------------------------

Languages can be leveraged to partition your navigation into different languages.

We currently support the following languages:

Arabic (ar)
-----------

Chinese (cn)
------------

Chinese (zh-Hant)
-----------------

English (en)
------------

French (fr)
-----------

German (de)
-----------

Indonesian (id)
---------------

Italian (it)
------------

Japanese (jp)
-------------

Korean (ko)
-----------

Portuguese (pt)
---------------

Portuguese (pt-BR)
------------------

Russian (ru)
------------

Spanish (es)
------------

Turkish (tr)
------------

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "navigation": {
        "languages": [\
          {\
            "language": "en",\
            "groups": [\
              {\
                "group": "Getting Started",\
                "pages": ["en/overview", "en/quickstart", "en/development"]\
              }\
            ]\
          },\
          {\
            "language": "es",\
            "groups": [\
              {\
                "group": "Getting Started",\
                "pages": ["es/overview", "es/quickstart", "es/development"]\
              }\
            ]\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }
    

* * *

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/navigation#nesting)

Nesting
------------------------------------------------------------

It’s important to note that you can use any combination of anchors, tabs, and dropdowns - either one can be nested within each other interchangeably.

This way, you can create a very complex navigation structure that is easy to manage.

Anchors

Tabs

Tabs with external anchors

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "navigation": {
        "anchors": [\
          {\
            "anchor": "Anchor 1",\
            "groups": [\
              {\
                "group": "Group 1",\
                "pages": [\
                  "some-folder/file-1",\
                  "another-folder/file-2"\
                  "just-a-file"\
                ]\
              }\
            ]\
          }\
          {\
            "anchor": "Anchor 2",\
            "groups": [\
              {\
                "group": "Group 2",\
                "pages": [\
                  "some-other-folder/file-1",\
                  "various-different-folders/file-2",\
                  "another-file"\
                ]\
              }\
            ]\
          }\
        ]
      }
    }

# Pages - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Core configuration

Pages

Each page is an MDX file, which combines Markdown content with React components to let you create rich, interactive documentation.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#page-metadata)

Page metadata
-------------------------------------------------------------------

Every page starts with frontmatter—YAML metadata enclosed by `---` at the beginning of your file. This metadata controls how your page appears and behaves.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#param-title)

title

string

required

The title of your page that appears in navigation and browser tabs.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#param-description)

description

string

A brief description of what this page covers. Appears under the title and improves SEO.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#param-sidebar-title)

sidebarTitle

string

A short title that displays in the sidebar navigation.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#param-icon)

icon

string

An icon next to your page title in the sidebar. Choose an icon from Font Awesome, Lucide, or use a custom URL. Configure your preferred icon library with the [icons library setting](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings#param-icons)
.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#param-tag)

tag

string

A tag that appears next to your page title in the sidebar.

Example YAML frontmatter

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: "About frontmatter"
    description: "Frontmatter is the metadata that controls how your page appears and behaves"
    sidebarTitle: "Frontmatter"
    icon: "book"
    tag: "NEW"
    ---
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#page-mode)

Page mode
-----------------------------------------------------------

Control how your page displays with the `mode` setting.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#default)

Default

If no mode is defined, defaults to a standard layout with a sidebar navigation and table of contents.

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: "Default page title"
    ---
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#wide)

Wide

Wide mode hides the table of contents. This is useful for pages that do not have any headings or if you prefer to use the extra horizontal space.

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: "Wide page title"
    mode: "wide"
    ---
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#custom)

Custom

Custom mode provides a minimalist layout that removes all elements except for the top navbar. Custom mode is a blank canvas to create landing pages or any other unique layouts that you want to have minimal navigation elements for.

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: "Custom page title"
    mode: "custom"
    ---
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#center)

Center

Center mode removes the sidebar and table of contents, centering the content. This is useful for changelogs or other pages where you want to emphasize the content.

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: "Center page title"
    mode: "center"
    ---
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#api-pages)

API pages
-----------------------------------------------------------

Create interactive API playgrounds by adding an API specification to your frontmatter, `api` or `openapi`.

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    openapi: "GET /endpoint"
    ---
    

Learn more about building [API documentation](https://mintlify.com/docs/api-playground/overview)
.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#external-links)

External links
---------------------------------------------------------------------

Link to external sites directly from your navigation with the `url` metadata.

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: "npm Package"
    url: "https://www.npmjs.com/package/mint"
    ---
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#search-engine-optimization)

Search engine optimization
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Most SEO meta tags are automatically generated. You can set SEO meta tags manually to improve your site’s SEO, social sharing, and browser compatibility.

Meta tags with colons must be wrapped in quotes.

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    "twitter:image": "/images/social-preview.jpg"
    ---
    

See [SEO](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/seo)
 for complete SEO metadata options.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/pages#internal-search-keywords)

Internal search keywords
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enhance a specific page’s discoverability in the built-in search by providing `keywords` in your metadata. These keywords won’t appear as part of the page content or in search results, but users that search for them will be shown the page as a result.

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    keywords: ['configuration', 'setup', 'getting started']
    ---
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

# PostHog - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Analytics

PostHog

Add the following to your `docs.json` file to send analytics to PostHog.

You only need to include `apiHost` if you are self-hosting PostHog. We send events to `https://app.posthog.com` by default.

Analytics options in docs.json

Example

Copy

Ask AI

    "integrations": {
        "posthog": {
            "apiKey": "YOUR_POSTHOG_PROJECT_API_KEY",
            "apiHost": "optional"
        }
    }
    

  

Enabling PostHog analytics will disable the analytics on the Mintlify dashboard.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/posthog#session-recordings)

Session Recordings
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You need to add the URL for your docs website to Posthog’s “Authorized domains for recordings” before you can receive session recordings. The option to add your URL is in Posthog’s project settings.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Segment\
\
Next](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/segment)

# Lists and tables - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Components

Lists and tables

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#lists)

Lists
--------------------------------------------------------

Lists follow the official [Markdown syntax](https://www.markdownguide.org/basic-syntax/#lists-1)
.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#ordered-list)

Ordered list

To create an ordered list, add numbers followed by a period before list items.

1.  First item
2.  Second item
3.  Third item
4.  Fourth item

Copy

Ask AI

    1. First item
    2. Second item
    3. Third item
    4. Fourth item
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#unordered-list)

Unordered list

To create an unordered list, add dashes (`-`), asterisks (`*`), or plus signs (`+`) before list items.

*   First item
*   Second item
*   Third item
*   Fourth item

Copy

Ask AI

    - First item
    - Second item
    - Third item
    - Fourth item
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#nested-list)

Nested list

Indent list items to nest them.

*   First item
*   Second item
    *   Additional item
    *   Additional item
*   Third item

Copy

Ask AI

    - First item
    - Second item
      - Additional item
      - Additional item
    - Third item
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#tables)

Tables
----------------------------------------------------------

Tables follow the official [Markdown syntax](https://www.markdownguide.org/extended-syntax/#tables)
.

To add a table, use three or more hyphens (`---`) to create each column’s header, and use pipes (`|`) to separate each column. For compatibility, you should also add a pipe on either end of the row.

| Property | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Name | Full name of user |
| Age | Reported age |
| Joined | Whether the user joined the community |

Copy

Ask AI

    | Property | Description                           |
    | -------- | ------------------------------------- |
    | Name     | Full name of user                     |
    | Age      | Reported age                          |
    | Joined   | Whether the user joined the community |
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Previous](https://mintlify.com/docs/image-embeds)
[CodeDisplay inline code and code blocks\
\
Next](https://mintlify.com/docs/code)

On this page

*   [Lists](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#lists)
    
*   [Ordered list](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#ordered-list)
    
*   [Unordered list](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#unordered-list)
    
*   [Nested list](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#nested-list)
    
*   [Tables](https://mintlify.com/docs/list-table#tables)

# Google Analytics 4 - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Analytics

Google Analytics 4

You will need to generate a new GA4 property to use with Mintlify. The data collected will go into the same project as your other Google Analytics data.

If you are using the old version of Google Analytics, Universal Analytics, you will still be able to generate a GA4 property. GA4 data is slightly different from UA data but still gets collected in the same project.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-analytics#how-to-connect-ga4-to-mintlify)

How to Connect GA4 to Mintlify
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-analytics#create-a-web-stream)

Create a Web Stream

You will need to create a web stream to get the Measurement ID to put into Mintlify.

Click the cog at the bottom left of the Google Analytics screen. Then click on Data Streams.

Create a Web Stream and put the URL of your Mintlify docs site as the stream URL.

Your Measurement ID looks like `G-XXXXXXX` and will show up under Stream Details immediately after you create the Web Stream.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-analytics#put-measurement-id-in-docs-json)

Put Measurement ID in docs.json

Add your Measurement ID to your `docs.json` file like so:

docs.json

Copy

Ask AI

    "integrations": {
        "ga4": {
            "measurementId": "G-XXXXXXX"
        }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-analytics#wait)

Wait

Google Analytics takes two to three days to show your data.

You can use the [Google Analytics Debugger](https://chrome.google.com/webstore/detail/google-analytics-debugger/jnkmfdileelhofjcijamephohjechhna?hl=en)
 to check analytics are enabled correctly. The extension will log to your browser’s console every time GA4 makes a request.

Preview links have analytics turned off.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Previous](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/fathom)
[Google Tag Manager\
\
Next](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-tag-manager)

On this page

*   [How to Connect GA4 to Mintlify](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-analytics#how-to-connect-ga4-to-mintlify)
    
*   [Create a Web Stream](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-analytics#create-a-web-stream)
    
*   [Put Measurement ID in docs.json](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-analytics#put-measurement-id-in-docs-json)
    
*   [Wait](https://mintlify.com/docs/integrations/analytics/google-analytics#wait)

# CI checks - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Version control and CI/CD

CI checks

CI checks are available on [Growth and Enterprise plans](https://mintlify.com/pricing?ref=docs-ci)
, an add-on for other plans, and for GitHub.

Use CI checks to lint your docs for errors, and give you warnings before you deploy.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#installation)

Installation
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

To begin, you will need to have followed the steps on the [GitHub](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/github)
 page.

For GitHub Apps, you can choose to only give permissions to a single repository. We highly recommend you do so as we only need access to the repository where your docs are hosted.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#configuration)

Configuration
-------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can configure the CI checks enabled for a deployment on the Mintlify dashboard by navigating to the ‘Add-Ons’ tab. There you can enable or disable the checks you’d like to run.

When enabling checks, you can choose to run them at a `Warning` or `Blocking` level.

A `Blocking` level check will provide a failure status if not passed, or changes are suggested.  

A `Warning` level check will never provide a failure status, even if there is an error or suggestions.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#when-do-they-run%3F)

When Do They Run?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CI checks are configured to run on commits to your configured deployment branch, or on pull requests against that branch.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#available-ci-checks)

Available CI Checks
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#broken-links)

Broken Links

Similarly to how the [CLI link checker](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/broken-links#broken-links)
 works on your local machine, we will automatically check your docs for broken links. To see the results of this check, you can visit GitHub’s check results page for a specific commit.

### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#vale)

Vale

[Vale](https://vale.sh/)
 is an open-source rule-based prose linter which supports a range of document types, including Markdown and MDX.

Mintlify supports automatically running Vale in a CI check, and displaying the results as a check status.

#### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#configuration-2)

Configuration

If you have a `.vale.ini` file in the root the content directory for your deployment, we will automatically use that configuration file. We will also automatically use any configuration files in your specified `stylesPath`.

Don’t have a Vale config or not sure where to get started? Don’t worry, Mintlify has a default configuration that will automatically be used if one is not provided.

Please note that for security reasons, we are unable to support any absolute `stylesPath`, or `stylesPath` which include `..` values. Please use relative paths and include the `stylesPath` in your repository.

#### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#packages)

Packages

Vale supports a range of [packages](https://vale.sh/docs/keys/packages)
, which can be used to check for spelling and style errors. Any packages you include in your repository under the correct `stylesPath` will be automatically installed and used in your Vale configuration.

For packages not included in your repository, you may specify any packages from the [Vale package registry](https://vale.sh/explorer)
, and they will automatically be downloaded and used in your Vale configuration.

Please note that for security reasons, we are unable to support automatically downloading packages that are not from the [Vale package registry](https://vale.sh/explorer)
.

#### 

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#vale-with-mdx)

Vale with MDX

Vale does not natively support MDX, but Vale’s author has provided a [custom extension](https://github.com/errata-ai/MDX)
 to support it.

If you’d prefer not to use this extension, we recommend the following lines in your `.vale.ini` file:

Copy

Ask AI

    [formats]
    mdx = md
    
    [*.mdx]
    CommentDelimiters = {/*, */}
    
    TokenIgnores = (?sm)((?:import|export) .+?$), \
    (?<!`)(<\w+ ?.+ ?\/>)(?!`), \
    (<[A-Z]\w+>.+?<\/[A-Z]\w+>)
    
    BlockIgnores = (?sm)^(<\w+\n .*\s\/>)$, \
    (?sm)^({.+.*})
    

To use Vale’s in-document comments, use MDX-style comments `{/* ... */}`. If you use the `CommentDelimiters = {/*, */}` [setting](https://vale.sh/docs/keys/commentdelimiters)
 in your configuration, Vale will automatically interpret these comments while linting. This means you can easily use Vale’s in-built features, like skipping lines or sections.

Copy

Ask AI

    {/* vale off */}
    
    This text will be ignored by Vale
    
    {/* vale on */}
    

If you choose not to use `CommentDelimiters`, but still choose to use Vale’s comments, you must wrap any Vale comments in MDX comments `{/* ... */}`. For example:

Copy

Ask AI

    {/* <!-- vale off --> */}
    
    This text will be ignored by Vale
    
    {/* <!-- vale on --> */}
    

Please note that these comment tags are not supported within Mintlify components, but can be used anywhere at the base level of a document.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Previous](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/gitlab)
[Preview deploymentsPreview changes to your docs in a live deployment\
\
Next](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/preview-deployments)

On this page

*   [Installation](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#installation)
    
*   [Configuration](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#configuration)
    
*   [When Do They Run?](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#when-do-they-run%3F)
    
*   [Available CI Checks](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#available-ci-checks)
    
*   [Broken Links](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#broken-links)
    
*   [Vale](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#vale)
    
*   [Configuration](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#configuration-2)
    
*   [Packages](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/ci#packages)

# SEO - Mintlify

[Mintlify home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/mintlify/logo/dark.svg)](https://mintlify.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Guides

SEO

The platform automatically generates most meta tags.

However, you can fully customize them by adding the `metatags` field to your `docs.json` or the page’s frontmatter.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/seo#global-meta-tags)

Global meta tags
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can set default meta tags by adding the `metadata` field to your `docs.json`.

Copy

Ask AI

    "seo": {
        "metatags": {
            "og:image": "link to your default meta tag image"
        }
    }
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/seo#page-specific-meta-tags)

Page-specific meta tags
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add your meta tags to the page’s metadata like so:

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    title: 'Your Example Page Title'
    'og:image': 'link to your meta tag image'
    ---
    

Meta tags with colons need to be typed with quotes around them when you put them in the page metadata.

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/seo#sitemaps)

Sitemaps
----------------------------------------------------------------

Mintlify automatically generates a `sitemap.xml` file and a `robots.txt` file. Simply navigate to `/sitemap.xml` to see your sitemap.

Only pages included in your `docs.json` are included by default. To include hidden links, add `seo.indexing` to your `docs.json`:

Copy

Ask AI

    "seo": {
        "indexing": all
    }
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/seo#disabling-indexing)

Disabling indexing
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to stop a page from being indexed by search engines, you can include the following in the [frontmatter](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/pages)
 of your page:

Copy

Ask AI

    ---
    noindex: true
    ---
    

You can also specify `noindex` for all pages in your docs by setting the `metadata.robots` field to `"noindex"` in your `docs.json`:

Copy

Ask AI

    "seo": {
        "metatags": {
          "robots": "noindex"
        }
      }
    

[​](https://mintlify.com/docs/settings/seo#common-meta-tags-reference)

Common Meta Tags Reference
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Below is a comprehensive list of meta tags you can add to your `docs.json`. These meta tags help improve your site’s SEO, social sharing, and browser compatibility.

You can preview how your meta tags will appear on different platforms using [metatags.io](https://metatags.io/)
.

Copy

Ask AI

    "seo": {
        "metatags": {
          "robots": "noindex",
          "charset": "UTF-8",
          "viewport": "width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0",
          "description": "Page description",
          "keywords": "keyword1, keyword2, keyword3",
          "author": "Author Name",
          "robots": "index, follow",
          "googlebot": "index, follow",
          "google": "notranslate",
          "google-site-verification": "verification_token",
          "generator": "Mintlify",
          "theme-color": "#000000",
          "color-scheme": "light dark",
          "format-detection": "telephone=no",
          "referrer": "origin",
          "refresh": "30",
          "rating": "general",
          "revisit-after": "7 days",
          "language": "en",
          "copyright": "Copyright 2024",
          "reply-to": "[email protected]",
          "distribution": "global",
          "coverage": "Worldwide",
          "category": "Technology",
          "target": "all",
          "HandheldFriendly": "True",
          "MobileOptimized": "320",
          "apple-mobile-web-app-capable": "yes",
          "apple-mobile-web-app-status-bar-style": "black",
          "apple-mobile-web-app-title": "App Title",
          "application-name": "App Name",
          "msapplication-TileColor": "#000000",
          "msapplication-TileImage": "path/to/tile.png",
          "msapplication-config": "path/to/browserconfig.xml",
          "og:title": "Open Graph Title",
          "og:type": "website",
          "og:url": "https://example.com",
          "og:image": "https://example.com/image.jpg",
          "og:description": "Open Graph Description",
          "og:site_name": "Site Name",
          "og:locale": "en_US",
          "og:video": "https://example.com/video.mp4",
          "og:audio": "https://example.com/audio.mp3",
          "twitter:card": "summary",
          "twitter:site": "@username",
          "twitter:creator": "@username",
          "twitter:title": "Twitter Title",
          "twitter:description": "Twitter Description",
          "twitter:image": "https://example.com/image.jpg",
          "twitter:image:alt": "Image Description",
          "twitter:player": "https://example.com/player",
          "twitter:player:width": "480",
          "twitter:player:height": "480",
          "twitter:app:name:iphone": "App Name",
          "twitter:app:id:iphone": "12345",
          "twitter:app:url:iphone": "app://",
          "article:published_time": "2024-01-01T00:00:00+00:00",
          "article:modified_time": "2024-01-02T00:00:00+00:00",
          "article:expiration_time": "2024-12-31T00:00:00+00:00",
          "article:author": "Author Name",
          "article:section": "Technology",
          "article:tag": "tag1, tag2, tag3",
          "book:author": "Author Name",
          "book:isbn": "1234567890",
          "book:release_date": "2024-01-01",
          "book:tag": "tag1, tag2, tag3",
          "profile:first_name": "John",
          "profile:last_name": "Doe",
          "profile:username": "johndoe",
          "profile:gender": "male",
          "music:duration": "205",
          "music:album": "Album Name",
          "music:album:disc": "1",
          "music:album:track": "1",
          "music:musician": "Artist Name",
          "music:song": "Song Name",
          "music:song:disc": "1",
          "music:song:track": "1",
          "video:actor": "Actor Name",
          "video:actor:role": "Role Name",
          "video:director": "Director Name",
          "video:writer": "Writer Name",
          "video:duration": "120",
          "video:release_date": "2024-01-01",
          "video:tag": "tag1, tag2, tag3",
          "video:series": "Series Name"
      }
    }

Assistant

Responses are generated using AI and may contain mistakes.
